< Text>
This requires an explanation.  I was going to give them 2 stars.  Their green sauce and the overall quality of the burrito I ate dragged them to 5 stars.  I could not give them less than 5 for how much I enjoyed that burrito, and have been thinking about it.  It was fantastic.
As you should be able to see from the photos, this place is well worn.  Not exactly in a good way.  Night club across the street, so kinda surprised it doesn't look worse actually.  Not a whole lot of parking, but it and the seating are accessible.  I originally ordered the eggs with shredded beef breakfast and was given it in a burrito.  Was not happy with the wrong order, even though it was like $.50 less.  But, was so surprised at how good it was, would be happy to return.  So, come here if you want some really excellent mexican fast food. Don't bring a first date, maybe at the end of a first date.  Best option may be getting it to go.
Parking and counter are accessible. Also should mention have come back a few times, quality has remained the same. Though they did mislabel 2 burritos one time, not a disaster, but annoying, and I'll still happily go back.</Text>

<rating>5<//rating>< review>
This Church has done a terrific job re-opening after the COVID-19 lockdown. Attending weekday morning Mass was easy and comfortable.  Their directions and signage are clean, simple and non intrusive.  The volunteers are kind, respectful and friendly.
We all followed the rules by respecting  social distancing, as well as wearing masks.  The 8:30 AM Weekday mass schedule seems to be well-attended and the church parking lot is accessible. Thanks to the priests and the volunteers for all the hard work.<//review>

At first the Church was good until certain homeless people dirtied the bathrooms and then eventually were having sex on the property after hours. Another homeless man exposed himself to the children who attend School there. Although they use this Church for a shelter for two weeks during the Winter, they still misuse the property by doing drugs outside the shelter area near the porta showers. I was homeless once, but i always respected the Church. Now because of what happened, the bathrooms have been locked to the parishioners unless you know the key code. It's a shame what some people do to ruin thing's for everyone else. This is God's house, please respect this house of worship! And finally, I've never had a problem with the Church at all.  They gave me and my girlfriend food and free coffee and doughnuts and were simply nice to us.</Review>

Come for the beer, stay for the trivia.  At least on Wednesday nights, when they host a pub quiz where you can test your bar trivia knowledge. Thomas Jefferson< /name>
<time>1622714262495</time><rate>5</rate>< review>
Brought my tahoe in for a simple smog.  Absolutely awesome staff! I forget then gentleman's name precisely, and I know I put their cars around here somewhere, but the Hispanic fellow, about 5'11-ish, heavy build, great dude! Superb customer service, his associate as well, the asian gentleman (again, sorry I forget their names).

Only needed to ask me a few questions and get the info from my vehicle and had the job done pretty quick. I was their last client for the day and I was having a hell of a time trying to prioritize a couple errands (gas cap seal was ineffective so I needed to replace first otherwise the machine would throw am immediate fault and fail the test) that nearly ended with me not being able to return for the day.

But the gentleman informed me that if I could try and make it back ASAFP, he would hold the shop open for about 15 minutes late (I think because he already had everything typed into the system and only needed to get the whip on the machine and run the test (which is relatively quick and easy process for the technician) but fortunately I was able to make it back with some time to spare and not require him to stay very late.

If you check my review log, you'll see that I don't write too many review, as I'm sure too many of us miss the opportunity to let people know how our experience was (believe me, there are MANY instances where negative reviews could clearly demonstrate that some employees absolutely trash a company's reputation or at least location, costing the business..  only God knows, how much, in the long run.

This is, for as long as I reside in the greater Sacramento area, my #1 Smog Spot! Thanks guys, stellar service and representation!<//review>

<Review>Heard a lot about the long waits and went in prepared to fight for a table. Surprisingly, we were seated on time and our appetizers popped out quickly. The calamari was fantastic but could use a bit more of the aioli. Unfortunately, some of the entrees were painfully average. The scallops were fantastic but the rest of the dish was meh. The huge chip on top needs a lot more salt. The mashed potatoes were bland and really could've used some flavoring. Perhaps rosemary or goat cheese.  The carrots felt off from the whole dish and the salmon was tasteless. I don't really know what the purple stuff was. It was ok for whatever it was. The green beans had a nice crunch to them and were refreshingly sweet and fresh. The filet mignon was AMAZING!!! Same words to the rest of the dish though. The dessert was ok. It didn't really fit together. The mousse has nuts in it (I presume walnuts) that weren't disclosed in the menu. The cocoa powder looks pretty but makes everything have a dry feeling in the mouth. The customer service was astounding. Blake was extremely friendly and was so on top of everything! Made us really feel at home. Overall great place!< /Review>< Rate>

< Review>
Excellent food. We opted for the pre fixe deal where you get a first course, main course and dessert for $55 (I think). I had the rack of lamb, wild mushroom streudel and creme brulee. My husband had their specials including cream of mushroom soup and crab crusted swordfish, and he got the citrus cheesecake for dessert. My lamb was juicy and cooked to perfection. The creme brulee was one of the best I've had. My husband enjoyed his meal also. They also made a good Malibu bay breeze. I was a little afraid of the negative reviews, but luckily, we saw no hint of rudeness, and the wait for the food was standard if not quicker than normal. We were there after 8pm on a Saturday. The place is small, and with everyone talking, it was loud. I didn't like that, but I'm not docking a star for it.</Review>

<Review>5/21/2014-Yelp Review

Upon dropping off the kittens at the  shelter for a check-up, I told the coordinator that if the kittens needed medical care that was outside the shelter's budgets, please call me and I would take the kittens to my vet for care. Dr. Hawkins looked at one kitten and euthanized it on the spot, without calling me or giving me the chance to get the kitten any treatment. I prefer this location over the one in Chino Hills. The selection while similar is made much better and is more flavorful. 1502659920000< /Time>
<Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
This has always been one of my favorite places. You can get just about anything. From Mexican food, to burgers, dogs, and chicken. Something for everyone.

Today, we got an order of chicken strips and fries, and fried zucchini, and an orange bang. The chicken was good. Thin strips. The breading is basic. No spices. The fries are awesome! My husband and I both like them a lot. Thin, shoestring. Cooked perfect.

The zucchini is the small, thin like fries. My hubby likes them like that. I prefer the big spheres. But they are really good here, anyway.

We've gotten burgers here, hot dogs. Burritos. Taquitos. All are Always so good. The breakfast burritos can feed 2. They are huge, delicious, and cheap for the amount you get.

Portion sizes are large. For a large zucchini, 3 chicken strips and fries, and a large drink, it was $15.01. That fed 2 of us, and we took some home.

The lobby is really big. They have a small game section for kids. Tvs playing. It was super busy, people coming and going today. So the lobby was pretty messy. People had to sit at dirty tables. Never saw anyone clean them.

No matter what you order, you will have a great meal here. Food comes out quickly, and drive thru is pretty quick every time.</review>

My wife and I went there for our anniversary dinner and had a fantastic time. The service was great including the free valet service. The restaurant is not small but has an intimate feel which makes it a great place for a romantic dinner.
All that said, I can't say enough about the quality of food. We had the prosciutto and the ravioli appetizers and the lamb and filet mignon for mains.
